          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="feature" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.vox.com/22321234/black-asian-american-tensions-solidarity-history">
            The history of tensions  and solidarity  between Black and Asian American communities, explained
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           How white supremacy tried to divide Black and Asian Americans  and how communities worked to find common ground.
          </p>

           </a>
          </h2>

          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.vox.com/2021/3/20/22340607/climate-change-strike-greta-thunberg-fridays-for-future-net-zero-emissions">
            Youth climate activists are back with new, sharper demands for countries and corporations
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           The Fridays for Future movement returned to spotlight a dangerous shortfall in climate action.

          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.vox.com/2021/3/20/22341888/iceland-dormant-volcano-erupted-fagradalsfjall-reykjavik">
            A 6,000-year-dormant Icelandic volcano just erupted  and its awesome
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           The eruption near Reykjavik followed months of earthquakes, and led to beautiful orange and red skies.
          </p>
          <div class="c-byline">
           <span class="c-byline-wrapper">
            By
            <span class="c-byline__item">

              </span>
             </a>

         <div class="c-entry-box--compact__body">
          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.vox.com/first-person/22338462/atlanta-shooting-georgia-spa-asian-american">
            How the history of spas and sex work fits into the conversation about the Atlanta shootings
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           Racism, misogyny, and anti-sex work stigma all intersect in the shootings that killed eight people, including six women of Asian descent.
          </p>
          <div class="c-byline">
           <span class="c-byline-wrapper">
            By
            <span class="c-byline__item">
             <a data-analytics-link="author-name" href="https://www.vox.com/users/Kimberly%20Kay%20Hoang">
              <span class="c-byline__author-name">
               Kimberly Kay Hoang
              </span>
             </a>
            </span>
           </span>

            </a>
           </span>

           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.vox.com/recode/22340453/planes-flights-pandemic-tsa-covid-19">
            The number of Americans getting back on planes istaking off
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">

           <div class="c-entry-box--compact__body">
            <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
             <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.vox.com/future-perfect/22334025/covid-19-coronavirus-pandemic-vaccines-cases-normal">
              When its safe to go back to normal
             </a>
            </h2>
            <div class="c-byline" data-cdata='{"timestamp":1616160600}' data-cid="site/byline-1616349770_3119_386952">
             <span class="c-byline-wrapper">
              By
              <span class="c-byline__item">
               <a data-analytics-link="author-name" href="https://www.vox.com/authors/german-lopez">
                <span class="c-byline__author-name">
                 German Lopez
                </span>
               </a>

    <script charset="utf-8" type="text/javascript">
     (function(){
  // load outbrain js
  function loadOutbrain(){
    var ref = document.querySelector("div.OUTBRAIN");

    var script = document.createElement('script');
    script.setAttribute('type','text/javascript');
    script.setAttribute('src', 'https://widgets.outbrain.com/outbrain.js');
    script.setAttribute('async', 'async');

    ref.appendChild(script);
  }

  // Disable on mobile and tablet screens
  // 880px is the upper bound for the `medium` breakpoint defined in UserAgent JS lib.
  var shouldDisable = false && screen.width <= 880;
  var scrollSubscriber = document.cookie.indexOf("scroll0=") > -1;
  var hymnalPreviewContent = !!(window.location.href.indexOf("concert_preview") > -1);

  if (!shouldDisable && !scrollSubscriber && !hymnalPreviewContent) {
    // first, set a timeout to loadOutbrain, in case no ads load in 5s
    // (i.e., blocked). once an ad has loaded, create a new timeout that
    // will load outbrain if openmic doesn't get loaded in 2s
    //
    var adBlockerTimeoutId = setTimeout(loadOutbrain, 5000);
    document.body.addEventListener('first_ad_rendered', function(){
      clearTimeout(adBlockerTimeoutId);
      var outbrainTimeoutId = setTimeout(loadOutbrain, 2000);
      document.body.addEventListener('playlistRendered', function(){
        clearTimeout(outbrainTimeoutId);
      });
    });
  }
})();
    </script>
